< Text>
THE SKIES THE LIMIT!!! What a location! This is the place to be for family brunches, cocktails at sunset and I look forward to knowing more. I just discovered The Riviera Hills Restaurant and Lounge and now have been there for Easter brunch buffet on the terrace with my family, casual dinner in the Lounge with my nine year old niece, and again on the terrace for a Sunday brunch with friends. Kevin in the Lounge is awesome and enthusiastic about sharing info about the area too. I've yet to know all the names, but I could see the staff's smiling eyes, (since all were wearing COVID masks). There is plenty of parking, I've made reservation for Easter, but the other times I just showed up and we were immediately seated. Clear Lake is a spectacular place, but I'm more impressed with the friendly people who I continue to meet from there. I look forward to my next visit. FYI, the brunch Eggs Benedict and endless champagne was pretty darn perfect. Worth every cent to enjoy this view and homemade food!<//Text>

< text>
The Philosophical Society Group meets every month for brunch the 2nd Sunday each month. We have the Riviera Hills Restaurant on the "every other month" rotation. We usually have a pretty good sized group of 30-35 people. Kevin (manager) is so accommodating and does a very good job getting us all served as fast as he can. His help are very professional/courteous and they see to all our needs! The Chef does a great job with the food! Tastes great and the food is presented very well!! The Riviera Hills Restaurant is VERY GOOD! I recommend you try it sometime soon!!
The views are awesome!!</text>

<review>Love this place. This restaurant has the best view in Lake county. Breathtaking sunsets so good they will have you and everyone else leaving the table to go outside and take a picture. Only open for dinner Thursday thru Sunday, this place is truly a hidden gym. Tucked away atop the hills of the Kelseyville Rivieras, this restaurant and clubhouse has a nice feel to it. You almost feel as though you are stepping into a movie sometimes because the ambience is so familiar and welcoming. The menu is a nice change of pace from a lot of the bar food you find around the area. The chef clearly knows what they are doing and you can tell from the menu and the different exquisite collections. Take the family to dinner or your significant other on a date here, you won't be sorry. The bar is a hoppin place on Saturday night and usually is packed with people dancing and a band playing live music. Do yourself a favor and check this place out!< /review>< pictures>

<GmapID>0x80e90ed5a7035aa1:0x60049221e211c34b< /GmapID><user_name>Daa Daa< /user_name>< Review>
10/5 stars.

Cheesy name, like many pho places.. not sure if there's a race somewhere to be the cheesiest. I digress.

Btw, I've tried many many Pho across SoCal. This is the best. No, this isn't a subjective opinion, if you don't like it.. there's something wrong with your taste buds.

Rich and creamy broth puts all other places to shame. Higher quality and delicious meat, the raw meat doesn't get hard and rubbery & the tripe was a bit cooked and doesn't stink. Absolute fan.

Okay, now the bad part. After you taste their pho, it's all downhill from there. You won't really be happy eating pho ever again. I'm serious.</Review>

<name>Jenny Dorman</name><Time>1575973739829< /Time><rate>5</rate>< review>
We loved this place - when you're hankering for both sushi AND Peruvian cuisine- this is the place to go!  Small intimate atmosphere - great for a small gathering or casual date.  You'll get the most bang for your buck either the off-menu Bento Box special - it cones with soup and rice.  I chose sashimi, spicy tuna roll, Lona Saltado (the venerable staple) and a vegetarian potato and asparagus side dish.  I chose the Fish Soup instead of Miso soup and it was delicious.  When dinning at any Peruvian restaurant, I always sample the Alfajor for dessert - a shortbread cookie filled with very light and delectable dulce de leche.  The cookie was perfect with some coffee.< /review>

I am 28 and have only been to a regular dentist 3 times in my life due to neglectful dad/step-mom, and then my own anxiety over doctors as an adult.

This dental office was compassionate, kind, extremely observant to my needs and made sure to talk me through the harder parts of my dental work. I was shown how to floss and brush properly, and was not shamed for being neglectful of my teeth in the past. I was educated on how to go forward, and had fun learning while getting my teeth fixed.

I had a total of 8 cavities done, antibacterial work for mid level gum disease, and a full mouth four quadrants of scaling and deep clean. They accomplished everything in under 5 hours, and I left feeling satisfied with the cost, customer service and the quality of technical work they did on my teeth.
